<p>Sittin'
on
a
bench
at
West
Town
Mall<br

He
sat
down
in
his
overalls
and
asked
me<br

waitin'
on
a
woman<br

nodded
yeah
and
said
how
'bout
you<br
/>
He
said
son
since
nineteen
fifty-two
I've
been<br
/>
Waitin'
on
a
woman</p>

























<p>When
I
picked
her
up
for
our
first
date<br
/>
I
told
her
I'd
be
there
at
eight<br
/>
And
she
came
down
the
stairs
at
eight-thirty<br
/>
She
said
I'm
sorry
that
I
took
so
long<br
/>
Didn't
like
a
thing
that
I
tried
on<br
/>
But
let
me
tell
you
son
she
sure
looked
pretty<br
/>
Yeah
she'll
take
her
time
but
I
don't
mind<br
/>
Waitin'
on
a
woman</p>

























<p>He
said
the
wedding
took
a
year
to
plan<br
/>
You
talk
about
an

man,
I
was
nervous<br
/>
Waitin'
on
a
woman<br
/>
And

like

men
do<br

And
said,
I'll

about
the

was
worth
it<br
/>
Waitin'
on
a
woman</p>

























<p>And
I
don't
guess
we've
been
anywhere<br
/>
She
hasn't
made

I
swear<br
/>

she

just
'cause

/>
Boy

just

/>
It'll

your

/>
Might
as

on
and
get
used
to
it<br
/>
She'll
take
her

'cause
you
don't

/>
Waitin'
on
a
woman</p>

























<p>I've
read
somewhere
statistics
show<br
/>
The
man's
always
the
first
to
go<br
/>
And
that
makes
sense
'cause
I
know

won't

/>
So
when
it
finally
comes
my
time<br
/>
And
I
get
to
the
other
side<br
/>
I'll
find
myself
a
bench,
if

got
any<br
/>
I
hope
she
takes
her
time,
'cause
I
don't
mind<br
/>
Waitin'
on
a
woman</p>
